\DoxyCodeLine{217 \textcolor{comment}{/* Platform-\/specific calling convention macros.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{218 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{219 \textcolor{comment}{ * Platforms should define these so that Vulkan clients call Vulkan commands}}
\DoxyCodeLine{220 \textcolor{comment}{ * with the same calling conventions that the Vulkan implementation expects.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{221 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{222 \textcolor{comment}{ * VKAPI\_ATTR -\/ Placed before the return type in function declarations.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{223 \textcolor{comment}{ *              Useful for C++11 and GCC/Clang-\/style function attribute syntax.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{224 \textcolor{comment}{ * VKAPI\_CALL -\/ Placed after the return type in function declarations.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{225 \textcolor{comment}{ *              Useful for MSVC-\/style calling convention syntax.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{226 \textcolor{comment}{ * VKAPI\_PTR  -\/ Placed between the '(' and '*' in function pointer types.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{227 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{228 \textcolor{comment}{ * Function declaration:  VKAPI\_ATTR void VKAPI\_CALL vkCommand(void);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{229 \textcolor{comment}{ * Function pointer type: typedef void (VKAPI\_PTR *PFN\_vkCommand)(void);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{230 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{231 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if defined(\_WIN32)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{232     \textcolor{comment}{/* On Windows, Vulkan commands use the stdcall convention */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{233 \textcolor{preprocessor}{    \#define VKAPI\_ATTR}}
\DoxyCodeLine{234 \textcolor{preprocessor}{    \#define VKAPI\_CALL \_\_stdcall}}
\DoxyCodeLine{235 \textcolor{preprocessor}{    \#define VKAPI\_PTR  VKAPI\_CALL}}
\DoxyCodeLine{236 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#elif defined(\_\_ANDROID\_\_) \&\& defined(\_\_ARM\_ARCH) \&\& \_\_ARM\_ARCH < 7}}
\DoxyCodeLine{237 \textcolor{preprocessor}{    \#error "{}Vulkan is not supported for the 'armeabi' NDK ABI"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{238 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#elif defined(\_\_ANDROID\_\_) \&\& defined(\_\_ARM\_ARCH) \&\& \_\_ARM\_ARCH >= 7 \&\& defined(\_\_ARM\_32BIT\_STATE)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{239     \textcolor{comment}{/* On Android 32-\/bit ARM targets, Vulkan functions use the "{}hardfloat"{} */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{240     \textcolor{comment}{/* calling convention, i.e. float parameters are passed in registers. This */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{241     \textcolor{comment}{/* is true even if the rest of the application passes floats on the stack, */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{242     \textcolor{comment}{/* as it does by default when compiling for the armeabi-\/v7a NDK ABI. */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{243 \textcolor{preprocessor}{    \#define VKAPI\_ATTR \_\_attribute\_\_((pcs("{}aapcs-\/vfp"{}})))}
\DoxyCodeLine{244 \textcolor{preprocessor}{    \#define VKAPI\_CALL}}
\DoxyCodeLine{245 \textcolor{preprocessor}{    \#define VKAPI\_PTR  VKAPI\_ATTR}}
\DoxyCodeLine{246 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{247     \textcolor{comment}{/* On other platforms, use the default calling convention */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{248 \textcolor{preprocessor}{    \#define VKAPI\_ATTR}}
\DoxyCodeLine{249 \textcolor{preprocessor}{    \#define VKAPI\_CALL}}
\DoxyCodeLine{250 \textcolor{preprocessor}{    \#define VKAPI\_PTR}}
\DoxyCodeLine{251 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}

\DoxyCodeLine{291 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define VK\_API\_VERSION\_PATCH(version) ((uint32\_t)(version) \& 0xFFFU)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{292 \textcolor{comment}{/* DEPRECATED: This define has been removed. Specific version defines (e.g. VK\_API\_VERSION\_1\_0), or the VK\_MAKE\_VERSION macro, should be used instead. */}}
